id=\"content\" class=\"site-content\" role=\"main\">\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<article id=\"post-42367\" class=\"post-42367 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-quotation category-quotes category-relationships tag-books-2 tag-philip-lopate tag-quotations tag-quote tag-relationships-2\">\n\t\n\n\t <header>\n                <div class=\"post-meta\" style=\"display:block;\">\n    <div class=\"post-date\">April 22, 2017</div>\n    \n</div>\n\n                <a href=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/learn-another-person/\"><h1>How Do We Learn Most About Another Person?</h1></a>\n            </header>    \n                   \n            <div class=\"entry\">\n               <div class=\"siderailsocialicons\">\n                <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/learn-another-person/&amp;t=How Do We Learn Most About Another Person?\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_facebook.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n                <a href=\"http://twitter.com/share?text=How Do We Learn Most About Another Person?&amp;url=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/learn-another-person/&amp;via=gretchenrubin; ?&gt;\" title=\"Share on Twitter\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_twitter.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n                <a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/learn-another-person/&amp;title=How Do We Learn Most About Another Person?\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_linkedin.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n               <a href=\"mailto:?subject=How Do We href=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/learn-another-person/\">\n                <img width=\"300\" height=\"225\" src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Phillip-Lopate-300x225.jpg\" class=\"attachment-featuredlarge size-featuredlarge wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Phillip-Lopate-300x225.jpg 300w, https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Phillip-Lopate.jpg 485w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\"></a></div>\n               \n                 <p>“You learn more about a person by living in his house for a week than by years of running into him at social gatherings.”</p>\n<p>–Philip Lopate, “Reflections on Subletting” in <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2oTzxHY\"><em><strong>Against Joie de Vivre: Personal Essays</strong></em></a></p>\n<p>Agree, disagree? I agree.</p>\n<p>What are other good ways to get to know someone? Travel together, work on a project together, meet his or her family, look at the photos on his or her phone…</p>\n \n                 \n                      \n\n\n\t\t\t\t                 <div class=\"footer-inside alsobox\"><h3>Also ...</h3>\n                 <ul class=\"also\">\t\n                 \t                 \t<li class=\"alsofieldsep\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><strong><img class=\"alignleft size-thumbnail wp-image-42117\" src=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/HappinessProjectpbcoverwithbursthighresoltion-150x150.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"150\" height=\"150\">If you're intrigued by the idea of doing your own \"happiness project</strong>,\" you may find it helpful to read my books <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/the-happiness-project/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>The Happiness Project</strong></em></a> and <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/happier-at-home/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>Happier at Home</strong> </em></a>-- all about happiness projects. To request a <strong>copy of my \"resolution chart\" to use as an example, as well as a blank chart to use yourself</strong>,&nbsp; it's <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/get-started/downloads/\"><strong>here</strong> </a>(scroll down).</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t                 </ul>\n  </div>\n                \n               \n\t\n\n</article><!-- #post-## -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t                        \n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<article id=\"post-42210\" class=\"post-42210 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-books category-clutter-busting category-family-2 category-habits-2 category-happiness-2 category-home category-interview category-popular-culture category-possessions tag-books-2 tag-clutter tag-energy tag-habits tag-home-2 tag-interview-2 tag-life-changing-magic-of-tidying-up tag-marie-kondo tag-order tag-possessions-2 tag-spark-joy\">\n\t\n\n\t <header>\n                <div class=\"post-meta\" style=\"display:block;\">\n    <div class=\"post-date\">April 20, 2017</div>\n    \n</div>\n\n                <a href=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/\"><h1>Observations from Marie Kondo about the Life-Changing Magic of Creating Good Habits.</h1></a>\n            </header>    \n                   \n            <div class=\"entry\">\n               <div class=\"siderailsocialicons\">\n                <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/&amp;t=Observations from Marie Kondo about the Life-Changing Magic of Creating Good Habits.\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_facebook.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n                <a href=\"http://twitter.com/share?text=Observations from Marie Kondo about the Life-Changing Magic of Creating Good Habits.&amp;url=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/&amp;via=gretchenrubin; ?&gt;\" title=\"Share on Twitter\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_twitter.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n                <a href=\"http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/&amp;title=Observations from Marie Kondo about the Life-Changing Magic of Creating Good Habits.\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_linkedin.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n               <a href=\"mailto:?subject=Observations from Marie Kondo about the Life-Changing Magic of Creating Good Habits.&amp;body=https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/\" title=\"Send this\narticle to a friend!\"><img src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/themes/gretchen-child/images/icon_email.png\" width=\"45\" height=\"45\"></a>\n                </div><div class=\"featuredimage\"><a href=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2017/04/marie-kondo/\">\n                <img width=\"300\" height=\"220\" src=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/kondo-book_0-300x220.jpg\" class=\"attachment-featuredlarge size-featuredlarge wp-post-image\" alt=\"Marie Kondo\" srcset=\"https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/kondo-book_0-300x220.jpg 300w, https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/kondo-book_0.jpg 545w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\"></a></div>\n               \n                 <p>Interview: <a href=\"https://konmari.com/\"><strong>Marie Kondo</strong></a>.</p>\n<p>It’s hard to exaggerate the influence that Marie Kondo has wrought with her blockbuster books <a href=\"https://alexa.design/2nyJBHE\"><em><strong>The Life-Changing Magic of Tidying Up</strong></em></a> and <a href=\"https://alexa.design/2nWknOK\"><em><strong>Spark Joy</strong></em></a>. The latter book takes its name, of course, from the question she urges us to ask ourselves, “<strong>Does this possession spark joy</strong>?”</p>\n<p>Her ideas about how to create order and fight clutter have helped countless people to give themselves more energy and peace. (You might ask, <strong>“How does something paradoxically give you more <em>energy</em> and give you more <em>peace</em>?</strong>” and I would say, <strong>“That is exactly the effect of clutter-clearing.</strong>“)</p>\n<p>The<em> New York Times</em> called her “perhaps the world’s only decluttering celebrity.” Absolutely!</p>\n<p>Even I don’t agree with everything that Marie Kondo prescribes (as I write about <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2016/05/disagree-marie-kondo-life-changing-magic-tidying/\"><strong>here</strong></a>), I’m a huge fan of her work. It’s practical, thought-provoking, and often surprising. For most of us, <strong>outer order contributes to inner calm</strong>, and her “KonMari method” resonates with many, many people.</p>\n<p>One thing I love is that alongside detailed instructions for how to fold a t-shirt, Marie Kondo makes observations like this: “<strong>Tidying is the act of confronting yourself; cleaning is the act of confronting nature</strong>.” Profound.</p>\n<p>In my books <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/the-happiness-project/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>The Happiness Project</strong> </em></a>and <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/happier-at-home/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>Happier at Home</strong></em></a> (can’t resist mentioning–both bestsellers), I write a lot about the role of possessions in building a happy life. It’s a fascinating area.</p>\n<p>I was thrilled to get the chance to ask Marie Kondo questions about happiness and good habits.</p>\n<h3><strong>Would you describe yourself as an <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/01/ta-da-the-launch-of-my-quiz-on-the-four-tendencies-learn-about-yourself/\">Upholder, a Questioner, a Rebel, or an Obliger</a>?</strong></h3>\n<p>In terms of tidying, I’m definitely an Upholder. I stay tidy because I feel that the effects ground me and allow my home to spark joy for my family and me.&nbsp; However, I’m not sure if I qualify as an Upholder in other aspects, as I’ll procrastinate submitting written work or sometimes show up late to get-togethers with friends or colleagues!</p>\n<p>Perhaps this makes me a <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/01/ta-da-the-launch-of-my-quiz-on-the-four-tendencies-learn-about-yourself/\"><strong>Questioner</strong></a>, as I’ll only do things if, when I ask myself: “<strong>Does it spark joy?</strong>” and the answer is “yes.” My very profession is centered on encouraging others to ask themselves: “Does it spark joy?” This must qualify me as a Questioner! [Yes, that sounds Questioner to me.]</p>\n<h3><strong>Does anything tend to interfere with your ability to keep your healthy habits? </strong></h3>\n<p>I usually go to bed early and wake up early with my kids, who are 18 and 5 months old. However, because I travel frequently for work, I’ll sometimes get jet-lagged. This can disrupt my sleep pattern for a couple of days after! When this happens, I get a little anxious that I am getting behind on work or missing out on time spent with my daughters while I try to catch up on rest.</p>\n<p><strong>Simply having children can interfere with healthy habits!</strong>&nbsp; For instance, before bed, I usually like to stretch and release any tension that may have developed over the course of the day. However, if one of my daughters cries or calls out for me, I’ll tend to them and, by the time they’re calmed down, I’m tempted to pass on stretching and head straight to bed.</p>\n<h3><strong>Have you ever been hit by a&nbsp;<em>lightning bolt</em>, where you changed a major habit very suddenly, as a consequence of reading a book, a conversation with a friend, a milestone birthday, a health scare, etc.?</strong></h3>\n<p>When I was 15, I would continually tidy my room, only to have it become cluttered again shortly after.&nbsp; <strong>This cycle contributed to so much stress that one day, I fainted</strong>. This breaking point made me realize that I was approaching tidying the wrong way.&nbsp; Instead of focusing on discarding things and approaching tidying as the removal of negativity, I realized that I needed to focus on finding and keeping things that spark joy.</p>\n<h3><strong>Do you embrace habits or resist them?</strong></h3>\n<p>For daily life, I try to keep to routines, but for work, I prefer variety. For example, I get new ideas by traveling and exposing myself to other countries’ cultures. I enjoy giving talks in a variety of locations, because it allows me to interact with different people and learn from their diverse perspectives.</p>\n<h3><strong>Has another person ever had a big influence on your habits?</strong></h3>\n<p><strong>My grandmother taught me the importance of tidying up even those places you don’t openly see</strong>, such as the insides of drawers and bureaus.&nbsp; She recognized the intrinsic beauty in belongings and took pride in their presentation in her home.&nbsp; When she dressed and accessorized, she applied the same philosophy to her personal appearance – everything mattered.&nbsp; I developed my initial respect for my belongings as a result of her influence.</p>\n \n                 \n                      \n\n\n\t\t\t\t https://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/pilesofpaper.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px\"></a></div>\n               \n                 <p><strong>One of my favorite things to do is to help my sister Elizabeth clear clutter</strong>. (If you want to listen to my all-time favorite episode, <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/04/podcast-10-special-episode-live-from-elizabeths-cluttered-closet/\"><strong>Very Special Episode 10</strong></a>, recorded from inside Elizabeth’s clutter-filled closet, listen <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/04/podcast-10-special-episode-live-from-elizabeths-cluttered-closet/\"><strong>here</strong></a>.)</p>\n<p>Our efforts included a good example of an important Secret of Adulthood:<strong> One of the worst ways to waste time is to do <em>well</em> something that we need not do <em>at all</em>.</strong></p>\n<p>I wonder: Is this a special problem for <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/01/ta-da-the-launch-of-my-quiz-on-the-four-tendencies-learn-about-yourself/\"><strong>Upholders</strong></a>? It’s probably not much of a problem for <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/happiness_project/2015/01/ta-da-the-launch-of-my-quiz-on-the-four-tendencies-learn-about-yourself/\"><strong>Questioners</strong></a>.</p>\n<p>Have you ever caught yourself pouring a lot of time and energy into something that, really, you didn’t need to bother to do at all?</p>\n<p>Check out <a href=\"http://www.smithandnoble.com/happier\"><strong>Smith and Noble</strong></a>, the solution for beautiful window treatments. Go to <a href=\"http://www.smithandnoble.com/happier\"><strong>smithandnoble.com/happier</strong></a> for <strong>20% off</strong> window treatments and free in-home or on-phone design consultations and free professional measuring.</p>\n<h2>Want to get in touch? 300px\"></a></div>\n               \n                 <p>“I became unique and I felt I was needed: my own eyes were needed in order that the copper-red of the beech could be set against the blue of the cedar and the silver of the poplars. When I went away, the landscape fell to pieces, and no longer existed for anyone; it no longer existed at all.”</p>\n<p>–Simone de Beauvoir, <a href=\"http://amzn.to/2oDe6uA\"><em><strong>Memoirs of a Dutiful Daughter</strong></em></a></p>\n<p>Does color exist when no one is there to see it? No. A beautiful realization.</p>\n \n                 \n                      \n\n\n\t\t\t\t                 <div class=\"footer-inside alsobox\"><h3>Also ...</h3>\n                 <ul class=\"also\">\t\n                 \t                 \t<li class=\"alsofieldsep\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><strong><img class=\"alignleft wp-image-39081 size-full\" src=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/07/happinessprojectcoverfullview.png\" alt=\"happinessprojectcoverfullview\" width=\"180\" height=\"180\">If you're intrigued by the idea of doing your own \"happiness project</strong>,\" you may find it helpful to read my books <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/the-happiness-project/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>The Happiness Project</strong></em></a> and <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/books/happier-at-home/about-the-book/\"><em><strong>Happier at Home</strong> </em></a>-- all about happiness projects. To request a <strong>copy of my \"resolution chart\" to use as an example, as well as a blank chart to use yourself</strong>,&nbsp; it's <a href=\"http://gretchenrubin.com/get-started/downloads/\"><strong>here</strong> </a>(scroll down).
